Educational News

Important News 144

Luo Jialun, President of National Central University, Scheduled to Take Office Today 145

Submitted to the Executive Yuan Yesterday

Detailed Presentation of Opinions on Reorganizing and Developing National Central University

And Statement of Term of Office Limited to One Year

Nanjing, 2nd - Luo Jialun is scheduled to take over as President of National Central University on the 3rd. The qualifying examination will be implemented as scheduled.

Nanjing, 2nd - Luo Jialun, the newly appointed President of National Central University, recently yielded to the exhortations of various parties, unable to bear to see National Central University stagnate for so long, leading to an unmanageable situation. Therefore, he upheld the spirit of accepting a mission in times of crisis and agreed to do his best to maintain it. Yesterday, he submitted a detailed report to the Executive Yuan, presenting his opinions on reorganizing and developing National Central University, requesting guidance on policies, and declaring that his term of office would be limited to a maximum of one academic year. The text of his submission is as follows:

Submitting a request for guidance on policies and declaration of term of office: If one does not worry about accepting the order of President of National Central University, one is either foolish or reckless. To see scholars who cherish their reputation shy away from the highest institution of national education is heartbreaking. Although Jialun is incompetent, does he not know how to cherish his reputation? It is only because various parties have held him responsible with righteousness, on the one hand, he cannot bear to see National Central University stagnate for so long, which will lead to an unmanageable situation, and on the other hand, considering the difficulties faced by the government and the future of the national cultural undertaking, he cannot bear to ignore the difficulties and dangers during the national crisis. Therefore, he does not hesitate to contribute his meager abilities, regardless of success or failure, and takes the spirit of accepting a mission in times of crisis to go. Moreover, the education undertaking is not absolutely impossible to do, and personal sacrifice is not something to be cherished. It depends on whether there is an educational ideal as a goal and whether there are steps to achieve this goal as a price for sacrifice. Jialun believes that managing National Central University should take forming an organic national culture as the ideal, so that the national university and the nation's survival have a close and unbreakable relationship. In the current national crisis, National Central University should especially bear the responsibility that the University of Berlin bore for Germany in the early and mid-19th century. With this advocacy, it becomes the academic style of the whole country. However, after the twists and turns of National Central University, if one wants to achieve this ideal, there must be practical steps. These steps can be divided into three periods. The first period is the stabilization period, which must be stable before it can be developed, and it must cultivate a spirit of academic research before it can be developed. Seek progress in stability. The second period is the enrichment period, striving for the concentration of talents and the increase of equipment. The third period is the development period, carrying out large-scale construction according to the planned plan to make it a modern university. Except that the first and second periods can be assumed to be combined into one year, the third period can last indefinitely. However, there must be the first period before the second period can be mentioned, and the second period must be passed before the third period can be reached. Otherwise, National Central University and a part of the nation's vitality will inevitably perish together in the midst of turmoil. If one wants to put National Central University on the right track, there are many factors, and the understanding of objective facts and the future of the nation by all parties is particularly important. Jialun hopes that the Executive Yuan will pay attention to three points in particular. First, the funds should be continued to be effectively maintained and guaranteed, and the full amount should be paid monthly according to the budget. Second, for the President of the University, please follow the established rules and give him special responsibility and deep trust. If there are any changes that should be made to the University Organization Law, please consider changing them during the reorganization period. At this time when we are striving for stability, we also hope to have the determination to help him solve difficult problems. Third, if there is a construction plan, please do your best to urge its implementation. If approved, Jialun is willing to sacrifice for an educational ideal. Success is the success of the national education undertaking, and failure is failure for martyrdom of his advocacy. Otherwise, he would not dare to increase his sins with his incompetent body. Moreover, Jialun has a request to make. Although Jialun has set three stages for the planning of National Central University, Jialun himself only dares to try to run it in the first stage. Please give him half a year first. If there is a factual necessity, then continue for another half year at most, to make it one academic year. When the time comes, he will resign resolutely, and must first search for virtuous and capable people to take over. However, within this period, Jialun will never have the intention of being a temporary official. He will hold on to public loyalty and courage, in addition to striving for reform, and he will also set a long-term plan for National Central University to promote its future development. If it is beneficial to the country, success does not have to be self-serving. Moreover, it is not convenient to take care of the Central Political School for a long time. For the sake of morality, Jialun cannot leave the political school for other places. If this stabilization period cannot be achieved or if funds cannot be supported, then any continued sacrifice by Jialun will be useless. He should immediately return what was entrusted to him by the Executive Yuan to the Executive Yuan, and ask it to make plans immediately to avoid leaving behind mistakes. His sincere words are respectfully presented, and he begs for guidance. He is extremely anxious. In addition to submitting a copy to the Ministry of Education, he respectfully presents it to the President of the Executive Yuan.

Jiangsu Education Department Promulgates Methods for Unifying Education and Training 146

(Continued)

Jiangsu Province County Secondary School Education and Training Integration Implementation Methods

(General Principles) Article 1: The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education has specially formulated these methods in order to unify education and training in provincial and county secondary schools. Article 2: The principles for formulating these methods are as follows: (1) Reform the divided system of teaching and nurturing; (2) Promote the common life of teachers and students, focusing on personality influence; (3) Based on the party's ideology, use teaching materials from various subjects to train students' thinking; (4) Correct the idea that teachers neglect the responsibility of nurturing. Article 3: Secondary school principals have the special responsibility to faithfully implement, lead, and supervise these methods. (Organization) Article 4: All secondary schools that combine senior and junior high schools shall establish one Director of Education and two Deputy Directors of Education under the principal. The original Directors of Senior High School, Director of General Studies, Director of Academic Affairs, Director of Moral Education, and Director of Normal School shall be abolished. Article 5: All secondary schools with separate senior and junior high school branches shall establish one Director of Education under the principal, and each senior and junior high school shall establish one or two Deputy Directors. All the original directors, except the Director of Affairs, shall be abolished. Article 6: Divide students in each grade into groups of 20 to 30 students (grades with 30 or more but less than 40 students, and those with more than 40 students, shall be divided into two groups). Each group shall have one tutor who is responsible for each grade, and one tutor shall be designated as the grade tutor. The original moral education staff and academic affairs staff shall be abolished. Article 7: The Director or Deputy Director of Education shall also serve as the grade tutor of one grade. The grade tutor shall also serve as the tutor of one group. Article 8: Tutors shall be appointed from full-time teachers. Grade tutors shall be selected by the principal from among the tutors. (Tasks) Article 9: In addition to performing the duties of the original Director of Academic Affairs and Director of Moral Education, the Director of Education shall also be responsible for the following tasks: (1) Planning the implementation of unified education and training; (2) Leading all tutors and students to live together; (3) Evaluating the service status of all tutors; (5) Reviewing various reports made by each tutor; (5) Convening and presiding over the Education and Training Conference. Article 10: The Deputy Director of Education assists the Director of Education and consults with the Director of Education to share the duties of the original Director of Academic Affairs and Director of Moral Education. If the Director of Education takes leave, the Deputy Director acts as his agent. If there are two or more Deputy Directors, the principal shall designate one to act as his agent. Article 11: The tasks of the grade tutor are as follows: (1) Diet, daily life, labor, recreation, and rest must be shared with the students of each grade; (2) Examine and guide the behavior, thoughts, and studies of the students of each grade at any time; (3) Participate in and guide the various extracurricular activities and autonomous organizations of students; (4) Hold at least one grade discussion per month and hold individual discussions at any time; (5) Convene all tutors and teachers of each grade to discuss the methods of connecting the teaching and training of the grade; (6) Attend the office, approve students' leave, and handle occasional incidents among students of each grade; (7) Collect and organize the monthly conduct reports made by the tutors of each grade, and fill out the grade reports of the students of each grade at the end of each semester; (8) Manage the discipline, service, hygiene, cleanliness, attendance, and inspection of the students of each grade. Article 12: The tasks of the tutor are as follows: (1) Convene students of each group for discussions once a week, and hold individual discussions at any time; (2) Fill out the conduct reports of the students of each group once a month and submit them to the grade tutor, and fill out special reports when necessary; (3) Review the life notes of the students in each group; (4) Guide the extracurricular reading of the students in each grade and the extracurricular activities and autonomous affairs of the students in each group; (5) Lead students to study on their own; (6) Attend Education and Training Conferences and various school gatherings and parades. (Conferences) Article 13: The meetings on education and training matters are divided into two types: Education and Training Conferences and Grade Tutor Conferences. The Education and Training Conference is held once a month, and the Grade Tutor Conference is held once a week. Temporary meetings may be convened when necessary. Article 14: The attendees of the Education and Training Conference are the principal, Director of Education, Deputy Director, Grade Tutor, Tutor, Party Ideology Teacher, Military Instructor, Scout Trainer, Director of Affairs, and School Doctor. The Director of Education convenes and presides over the meeting. Article 15: The attendees of the Grade Tutor Conference are the Director of Education, Deputy Director, and Grade Tutor. The Director of Education convenes and presides over the meeting. If necessary, relevant tutors or other personnel may be invited to attend. Article 16: In addition to the matters that should be discussed at the original Academic Affairs Conference and Moral Education Conference of each school, the main items for discussion at the Education and Training Conference are as follows: (1) Discuss and decide on the education and training plan and its implementation plan; (2) According to the plan, discuss and decide on the central work of education and training for each period, and review the implementation results of the central work of the previous period; (3) Review various rules and forms regarding education and training matters; (4) Discuss major occasional incidents regarding students; (5) Review student achievement reports at the end of each semester; (6) Discuss the selection of teaching materials and their methods of use to achieve the integration of teaching and training; (7) Discuss matters submitted by the principal and other meetings; (8) At the beginning of each semester, stipulate the guiding matters for student autonomy and extracurricular activities, and assign guiding personnel; (9) Other matters regarding education and training. Article 17: The main items for discussion at the Grade Tutor Conference are as follows: (1) Report on the actual situation of the implementation of central work in each grade, exchange opinions, and decide on the steps to be taken this week; (2) Handle matters of mutual relations between grades and discuss all difficult problems regarding education and training; (3) At the beginning of each semester, draft a list of seating arrangements and groupings for students' food, lodging, self-study, etc., and submit it to the Education and Training Conference for approval and implementation; (4) Discuss other matters regarding education and training that should be recommended. (Supplementary Provisions) Article 18: Full-time teachers who serve as tutors shall receive an additional monthly salary of a certain amount. Tutors who also serve as grade tutors shall receive an additional monthly salary of a certain amount. The monthly salary of the Director and Deputy Director of Education shall be determined by each school with reference to the salary of the original directors. Article 19: Each secondary school shall formulate detailed plans and rules for the implementation of these methods and submit them to the Department of Education for approval and implementation. Article 20: The principal of each school shall submit a detailed report on the results of the trial implementation of these methods to the Department of Education for verification at the end of each semester. Article 21: These methods shall be promulgated and implemented by the Department of Education and reported to the Provincial Government for submission to the Ministry of Education for record. (End)

Local News

Municipal Education Bureau Rectifies Private Schools 147

(Central News Agency) The Municipal Education Bureau has repeatedly submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval to extend the deadline for private schools in the city to register until the end of June this year, and has issued a notice to all schools to strictly urge them to apply within the deadline. Now that the deadline has passed, the bureau intends to strictly ban those who have not complied with the regulations. The news obtained is as follows:

▲Banning Private Schools That Have Not Applied for Registration: As of the deadline at the end of June this year, the number of private schools in the city that have been approved for registration is 60 middle schools and 153 elementary schools. The number of those approved for trial operation is 8 middle schools and 78 elementary schools. The number of those that need to be improved is 1 middle school and 64 elementary schools. The number of those approved to establish schools is 32 middle schools and 192 elementary schools, which are already in progress. The number of those who have submitted applications for registration is 24 middle schools and 112 elementary schools. In addition, there are still 7 middle schools and 61 elementary schools that have not complied with the regulations on private schools to apply for registration. The bureau has compiled a list and sent letters to the Public Security Bureau, the Special Zone Court, and the patrol station to strictly ban them.

▲Schools That Have Not Been Approved for Establishment May Not Enroll Students: The bureau recently published a notice in the newspaper stating that if a private individual or private legal person wants to establish a middle or elementary school in the city, they should comply with the regulations on private schools and apply for approval in order before they can open and start enrolling students. New specialized schools above the junior college level should be submitted to the bureau in order for review and transfer to the Ministry of Education for approval. Otherwise, they will be immediately banned, and the bureau has sent letters to major newspapers to refuse to publish enrollment advertisements.

Shanghai Municipal Council Allocates Subsidies to Private Schools 148

In order to promote education, the Shanghai Municipal Council has specially designated funds in the budget to subsidize appropriate private middle and elementary schools in the concession. Due to certain reasons, the payment of this subsidy to Chinese private schools was suspended last year. This year, with the assistance of the Municipal Education Bureau, the Shanghai Municipal Council reviewed the applications of various schools for subsidies and selected a Chinese committee within the bureau to formulate implementation methods and review the subsidies and the amounts to be given. Subsequently, it was decided to grant subsidies to a total of 57 schools, divided into four categories: nine schools in category A, sixteen schools in category B, fifteen schools in category C, and seventeen schools in category D. The total annual subsidy is 82,500 taels of silver, the highest of which is 14,000 taels for the YMCA Middle School, and the lowest is 150 taels for certain elementary schools. Now, the amount for the first half of the year is being issued first, totaling 41,250 taels. This case has been approved for implementation by the board of directors of the Shanghai Municipal Council at its meeting this Wednesday. However, before the next payment, the Shanghai Municipal Council may still review it again. The schools that receive this subsidy should use it to improve the school's facilities, and the sanitation facilities should be handled first to emphasize hygiene. The sanitation conditions of each school are also inspected by personnel from the Shanghai Municipal Council Health Department to facilitate improvement. The financial reports submitted by each school have also been deemed satisfactory by the Shanghai Municipal Council Finance Department. As for the private schools of various foreign nationals, the subsidy for the first half of this year has also been allocated, and the distribution method is roughly the same as last year.

Establishment of the National Studies Training Institute 149

The Chinese Cultural College was planned to be established by Wang Shengshan, chairman of the board of directors of Guanghua University, Professor Zhang Shoujian, Li Xuchuan, Hu Pu'an, Feng Bingnan, Wu Zhongwen, etc. The preparatory office was established at 55 Huayuanfang, Jinshenfu Road, and has been in existence for more than a year. In addition to surveying 118 mu of land for the campus on Meiren Peak in Hangzhou, engaging in the construction of school buildings, and starting to raise a fixed fund of 300,000 from Nanyang and other places, recently, due to the feeling that there are many people in society, school students, and those who are interested in studying national studies who lack the foundation of national studies and have no opportunity to study, the National Studies Training Institute was specially established. Free Talk

Sayings of the 93-Year-Old Ma Xiangbo

Not a Single Bullet Allowed to Be Wasted Internally 161

The other day, the Grand Alliance to Abolish Internal War Assembly appointed Ma Xiangbo and fifteen others as honorary members. Recalling the previous time Elder Ma replied to the letter initiating this alliance, he certainly supported this righteous cause from the beginning, as Elder Ma had long understood it. It's a pity that due to health reasons, he was unable to participate in this meeting.

When Elder Ma received the announcement initiating the Grand Alliance to Abolish Internal War, he told me to write a reply, roughly saying:

[Didn't I publish a warning to the people last year? I already expressed that from now on, I hope that genuine public opinion will be thoroughly and fully expressed. Unless permitted by public will, not a single bullet should be wasted internally; externally, not a single bullet should be spared! Now that someone has proposed a plan for implementation, quickly reply to the initiators, saying that I gladly agree!]

Therefore, I was reminded of two things.

One is Elder Ma's description of the astonishing speed with which Japan copied the American pistol. He told the visiting Japanese reporter that an American warship sailed to Japan around the time of the Meiji Restoration. The Americans on board gave the Japanese on shore two gifts: a pistol and an umbrella. Unexpectedly, the next day, the Japanese returned the copied pistol and umbrella, gift for gift, to the Americans. Elder Ma was not surprised by the Japanese ability to imitate. He was amazed that we still cannot fully utilize domestic products and have our own people manufacture modern new-style guns and cannons.

One is Elder Ma's description of the astonishing speed with which Japan copied the American pistol. He told the visiting Japanese reporter that an American warship sailed to Japan around the time of the Meiji Restoration. The Americans on board gave the Japanese on shore two gifts: a pistol and an umbrella. Unexpectedly, the next day, the Japanese returned the copied pistol and umbrella, gift for gift, to the Americans. Elder Ma was not surprised by the Japanese ability to imitate. He was amazed that we still cannot fully utilize domestic products and have our own people manufacture modern new-style guns and cannons.

One is that Elder Ma, reading the newspaper, often saw news of gunpowder depots being carelessly lost, and couldn't help but sigh: [There are people receiving salaries, but no one taking responsibility. That's why China is in such a mess! For example, with gunpowder, there is no one with scientific knowledge to take care of it, letting those irresponsible people destroy it all!]

One's Own Affairs 162

— Xu Jinwen

The Sad People of Shanghai

Su Dongpo said: [An old man, seeing through the matter of life and death, instructed his sons on his deathbed, saying, "It is only appropriate to rise at the first fifth watch," and also said, "Only at the fifth watch are one's own affairs to be attended to. One's own affairs are those that can be taken away at the time of death." According to Confucian teachings, these "own affairs" are the great path of self-cultivation and establishing one's destiny, so emphasis is placed on the fifth watch, which is what Mencius called the "vitality of dawn."] Ordinary people are deluded by fame and fortune, indulge in licentiousness and extravagance, and most of what they think and do is to harm others and benefit themselves. Only when midnight dreams return and the morning bell faintly sounds, when yin reaches its end and yang begins to rise, do evil thoughts subside and good intentions suddenly arise. Those with great wisdom are often able to hold onto this spark of inspiration, guard it and not lose it, expand it and fill it, so that the mind is clear and mundane worries gradually disappear. [The inner ruler is at peace,] and life and death are both forgotten. Even in the final five minutes, one does not feel the slightest regret. Even after death, one can, with the power of pure and karma-free energy, be reborn in the Western Paradise. This is what is meant by "that which can be taken away at the time of death," truly one's own affairs.

Why am I writing this roundabout statement? Because living in a place like Shanghai, a few friends, casually playing a few rounds, chatting a few words, or running around, eating here and playing there, muddledly stirring things up, unknowingly, it becomes two or three o'clock. Moreover, important office hours and appointments with friends are mostly after three or four o'clock in the afternoon. If one gets up at eight or nine o'clock and goes out to visit friends, it is mostly disturbing their sleep. What fifth watch? What dawn? The situation and the facts are that as soon as one closes one's eyes, the most precious time of the day, twelve hours, passes by in sleep. So-called "own affairs" are simply impossible to contemplate, let alone talk about practicing them. Yet it is precisely the people of Shanghai who are the busiest, so busy all their lives that they have never managed to take care of a few things for themselves. Therefore, I feel that the people of Shanghai (in fact, not just Shanghai) are pitiable! Especially, I feel that Shanghai society is terrifying!

However, I myself am one of the people of Shanghai…

Going to Teahouses 163

— Qing Ping

Living in the inland areas, unlike the gentlemen of the cities, they know how to seek enjoyment. Their pastime, when they are idle, is only [going to teahouses].

Therefore, every afternoon, the teahouses are always crowded with teahouse patrons who cannot be dispersed. Not all of these people necessarily have jobs, right?

If we say that everyone has a job, then they should not abandon their proper duties and come to this place to chew on idle gossip. Because not doing proper things and secretly indulging in ease is the most unacceptable thing.

Moreover, the majority of this group is still those unemployed people who have been squeezed out of society.

Friends, friends who love going to teahouses, look back and see if this era is one where you can idly [go to teahouses]!

Freedom of Marriage 164

— Bai Shi

Easy to Separate and Reunite, Simple Handiwork

Two days after last year's Christmas, a new neighbor moved into our side building. The male owner was about fifty years old, as thin as a tree trunk. The female owner was about twenty years old, completely a model of a young girl. It is said that their relationship was neither father-daughter nor father-in-law and daughter-in-law, but truly husband and wife.

Not long after, the Shanghai Incident broke out. The house we lived in happened to be a very close neighbor of the barbed wire, so everyone was busy fleeing. The sister-in-law in our side building was of course no exception. When everyone became tired of fleeing this March, they gradually moved back. The sister-in-law in our side building was of course no exception, doing the work of an old swallow recognizing its nest.

But a new thing was discovered. Our side building's sister-in-law fled with her husband, who was as thin as a tree trunk, but when she returned, she came back with a short, fat man of about thirty. It is said that her husband had gone to Hankou, and this short, fat man was [recruited] by her husband.

One evening in early July, a sudden marital conflict broke out in the side building. According to the short, fat man, it was because she was not behaving as a wife should; according to the side building's sister-in-law, it was because he was not providing for her. Crying, shouting, fighting, it lasted all night. The next day, the two went out together. Since then, for a week, the side building's sister-in-law did not return. The landlady went to inquire with the maid in the side building. The maid only said she didn't know.

On the afternoon of the eighth day, a car honked loudly at the door, and the side building's sister-in-law returned. Strangely, she was followed by a young man in a very stylish Western suit. The next day, our landlady secretly asked the side building's maid, [Who is the young man that your madam brought back yesterday?] The maid smiled and said: [He is our young master, our madam's husband.]

Do You Want Inheritance? 165

— Zi

Inspired by Li Minghui and Zheng Guoyou

A friend from Hong Kong came to Shanghai, and in idle conversation, he mentioned the lawsuit between Li Minghui and Zheng Guoyou. He said: Zheng Guoyou's instigation of Feng Deqian's death is probably not wrong. Fortunately, English law emphasizes evidence. The murderer is Zheng's chauffeur, who has still not been caught. Then, perhaps Zheng Guoyou's crime will not be established, which is also possible. Zheng is a wealthy man; he has several million in assets, all inherited from his father. He once brought 80,000 yuan to Shanghai, and because he was infatuated with Miss Li, he managed to spend it all in a few months. When he returned, he had to borrow money to travel. This time, the song and dance troupe went to Nanyang. He and Miss Li are old acquaintances, so naturally, they are especially intimate. However, why does Miss Li not accept being promoted by others? She is unwilling to grow old with Zheng Guoyou, but instead becomes close to Feng Deqian, who has no property? I asked my friend if Zheng's appearance was inferior to Feng's. He said not necessarily. Because Zheng Guoyou is also a handsome young man in this turbid world, his appearance may not be inferior to Feng Deqian's. If that's the case, then it's really as the Buddha said, the karma is predetermined.

After listening to my friend's words, I couldn't help but become pedantic. I thought: If Zheng Guoyou didn't have so much inheritance, he wouldn't have had this kind of distress. At the age of twenty-two, he is in the era of striving for learning. If he were a commoner, he might have become a promising young man in the future. Now that he has so much inheritance, eating without worry, it is exactly the ancient saying that "when one is full and warm, one thinks of licentiousness." Isn't this the harm that inheritance has brought him? There are many people like Zheng Guoyou in the current society, but they don't commit such shocking acts, so there's no way to investigate. But what I know is already a lot.

What I said in this section is too vague, but because of the inheritance, this promising young man fell into the trap of love and ended up in legal trouble. I heard that the new film "Revival of the National Soul" by the star [company] depicts the evils of inheritance at the beginning. All those who are already parents and those who are not yet parents should go and see it.

Silver Threads (3) 166

— Jiang Hongjiao

(Two)

Everyone in the town hates Yuan the Madman, but the situation when everyone in the town had fled empty during the war, and only a madman was left in the town, can only be described by Yuan the Madman. Therefore, after the war was over, everyone went to ask Yuan the Madman, wanting to get some real information about the war zone, especially Mr. Zhu Bofang, the local tyrant-gentry-style municipal committee member, because his responsibility was to make a memorial to report the situation at that time to the local government.

The general situation described by Yuan the Madman was like this - he described it unsystematically, but very vividly, making all the residents of the town very excited and慷慨.

[The small stone bridge outside the town has been dismantled by our army, and a temporary wooden bridge has been built. Trenches have been dug along the river bank. This trench leads directly to the Zhao family bamboo garden in front. A small steel cannon is hidden in the bamboo garden. Several gunners are squatting there day and night, lying still. At that time, I heard the rumbling of cannons and the rattling sound of airplanes overhead, especially the machine guns, continuously firing, deafening my ears.

I couldn't escape the town at that time, and later I couldn't even get another chance to leave. But later I decided not to escape, wanting to see what war really looks like. At first, none of the troops in the town knew that I was still hiding in my house, until one day, I myself didn't know how I ended up running into the trenches. They were very shocked and surprised. Perhaps my madness proved that I was not an enemy spy, otherwise I would have been shot by the army long ago. They all held me down, not allowing me to move, not allowing me to shout, not allowing me to look up and look ahead. At that time, there were scattered gunshots in front, followed by whistling sounds passing over my head.

[The whole town was as silent as death, not even the sound of people or dogs could be heard, but the sound of gunfire was a big exception. Once, I was a little panicked. When I was cooking at home, I suddenly heard a huge sound, like the sky falling and the earth cracking. The house I was living in was shaking as if it was about to collapse. The bowls and plates on the table were shaking to the ground. I hurried out of the house to escape! God! The house where Second Sister Yu lived had completely collapsed. The damned enemy planes, there were three in total, were still circling in the sky.

[A soldier told me that there were only fifty-two brothers in the entire town's army. Once, the front line collapsed, and this small town was very tight, but our Regiment Commander Yuan strictly ordered us not to retreat. Our company commander repeatedly asked for help, requesting that the cannons be moved back, but Regiment Commander Yuan did not allow it, only adding a machine gun to be deployed in the bamboo garden.

Financial and Gold Markets Fluctuate 167

▲ Small Fluctuations, Dropped Two Taels The Gold Market yesterday was still full of incessant waves, rising and falling, with a total fluctuation of nine taels throughout the day. The market situation was unpredictable and unstoppable, finally falling slightly by two taels. The opening was slightly soft, likely because the silver market was flat in England and down in America. Although the forward market also fell again, it was not affected, really because the current situation was not without influence. Later it weakened further, and with the exchange rate firm, Chinese merchants rushed to cover their short positions. Further, because large institutions were actively buying, with a certain bank trading USD for cash, people's confidence was easily improved, and the market rose steadily, suddenly breaking through the 710-tael mark. Later, because rumors were rife and the local situation deteriorated, selling pressure spread. When the exchange rate turned from firm to weak, the price of gold plummeted, from a range of 712 taels to 703.4 taels. In short, people were terrified and uncertain. The detailed situation of the market before and after is described as follows:

▲ Morning Market Low then High From an early opening of 705.5 taels for October, slightly lower by 0.04 taels. The expected continued narrowing of the margin from the day before did not materialize. However, with American silver down 0.25 from both public and private banks, and the exchange rate flat in England and down in America, the gold price stabilized. Then it increased to 706 taels. However, sellers were active, with Hengxingyuan, Hengchangyong, and others selling aggressively. Because the exchange banks initially bought October at 68.75, the gold price immediately fell more than 3 taels, with a quick reversal of over 1 tael, reaching 702.8 taels at a little after 9:10. Soon after, Zhenchangxiang came to buy, and banks dealt for September at 702.5, immediately adding 1 tael. At 9:30 it was 704.5. HSBC's listing did not change, and with Dalian Gang and others selling, it became 703.5 taels. After a while, Zhifeng, Yongyi, and Fengyong bought in, reaching 705 taels at 10:15. But with HSBC issuing September USD at 702.5, and Hengxingshunli, Hengyu, and others selling aggressively, it fell back 2 taels, reaching 702.9 taels close to 11:00. Suddenly, the Central Bank opened with cash, immediately becoming popular. Jichang, Bingxing, and others bought like clouds. At 11:30 it was 709.2 taels, with fluctuations of no more than 1 tael in between. At this time, Tongtaichang, items, etc. came to sell, and only a few minutes apart, it was suppressed by a little over 1 tael, to 707.6 taels. Afterwards, the market situation was quite good. Jichengfeng Yong covered by selling USD, and Fuyu entered the market to buy. By the afternoon closing it was 710.2 taels. China Bank absorbed this month's USD at 700.625, and the previous order of this month at 704.375 was available for sale. Tongtaichang and others continued to enter, so it continued to rise by 1 tael, to 711.2 taels (unofficial market).

▲ Afternoon Market Softening, Colors Gradually Clear The afternoon market opened at 711.3 taels, then went from 710 taels to 711.9 taels, with Shunli and others buying in. Later, because China Bank released October USD at 701.875, December at 700.5, HSBC released this month's English gold at 704.375, and the market like Zhaofeng and Chang were selling aggressively, it immediately retreated to 708.8 taels. Suddenly it increased to 710 taels, because at a little after 2:30, the exchange banks had changed to narrowing the margin by 0.125 USD to 702.5. But the domestic market did not show good signs. September English gold was traded for half a penny. Mumbai sold December at 706.875. Instantly, rumors flourished in the market, and people's confidence immediately plummeted. The price fell by 3 taels, and Zhifengyong and others tried hard to sell. At 3:20 it fell to 707.5 taels, then it increased to 708.3 taels. After 3:30 the atmosphere was particularly bad. Zhifengyong, Zhaofengchang, and others sold vigorously, but the buyers were unhappy, and the exchange rate became weaker. Therefore, the price of gold plummeted by 5 taels, but the position was less than 1 tael. At a little after 4:20 it was only counted at 703.3 taels. Soon after it was 704.1 taels. By the closing at 4:30 it was 703.9 taels, a small decrease of two taels compared to the previous day. It then rose by about 2 taels, to 704.78 taels, then generally individual positions were covered. According to the maximum of 711.9 taels and the minimum of 702.8 taels in one day, there was a fluctuation of 9.1 taels. The open interest increased by 9 taels. The initial listed price was 777 taels, with a margin of 72-73 taels, 67 taels at noon, and in the afternoon the USD was changed to a small margin of 0.25, so it was also changed to 784 taels, with a margin of 74 taels, to 81 taels later, more margin than the previous day by about 10 taels. The ledgered price was 710 taels in the morning market and 704 taels in the afternoon market, with a water payment of 10 taels. There was already double closing at 704 taels in the afternoon market.

Silk and Tea: Changes in Autumn Silkworm Rearing in Zhejiang Province 181

In Zhejiang Province, in the areas of Hangzhou, Shaoxing, Huzhou, and Jiaxing, the feeding of silkworm eggs for the autumn silkworm season is relatively smooth this year. There are also instructors making rounds to provide guidance, so the silkworm eggs are progressing well. However, purchasing leaves is difficult, and leaf prices are relatively high. The damage from the previous thunderstorms was minimal. Currently, the early silkworms have already gone onto the frames, while the late silkworms are still in their third molt and opening their leaves. However, continuous strong winds and rain in recent days, coupled with a sudden drop in temperature, have caused changes in the silkworms. The early silkworms on the frames are spinning silk slowly, while the late silkworms are showing diseases such as white muscardine, yellowing, and blackening. The silkworm farmers are all worried.

The main markets for various goods in the market are listed below:

▲Galvanized Iron Sheets Becoming Increasingly Scarce: Various groups rushed to purchase galvanized iron sheets yesterday, leading to a decrease in inventory. Standards are increasingly strong. Even unpopular sizes like #24 rose accordingly, with asking prices of 10 taels per dan. #26 and #28 are also scarce, with market prices estimated at 11 taels and 5 qian. It is said that the arrival of the next batch of goods is far off, raising concerns about supply shortages in the market.

▲British Steel Plates Cannot Recover: Since the drop in prices for British steel plates after the spring in Fujian, there has been no hope of recovery to this day. Although the Iron Industry and Metals Associations have both expressed discussing price increases, no practical way to do so could be found and the market's price plans proved illusory. As a result, market sales continue to shrink, leading to a situation where recovery is unlikely. Currently, 2.5 li sheets are estimated at 8 taels per dan, 5 li sheets at 5 taels and 2 qian, 7.5 li sheets at 4 taels and 9 qian, and 1 fen sheets at 4 taels and 6 qian, all down by 2-3 qian compared to the previous market. If this continues, the future will be precarious.

▲Ribbed Steel Crisis Remains: Ribbed steel is currently estimated at 64-5 taels, lacking buyers. However, compared to the cost for other merchants, that is still a loss of over 10 taels. Although merchants in this business all want to maintain prices, the environment is bad, and foreign firms are selling off inventory, so the market's future is not optimistic. Moreover, recent overseas pricing is reported to be low, so the Shanghai crisis has not yet passed. Maintaining the recent situation can already be considered fortunate.

▲New Lead Wire Internal Demand Exhausted: The quantity of new lead wire opened yesterday was high, at 500-600 dan. However, the market price is strong on the outside but weak on the inside. Currently, #16 to #20 is estimated at 13 taels and 2.5 qian per dan, and #21 to #25 is estimated at 18 taels and 5 qian. However, actual transactions are down by 3-4 qian. It is said that the reason for the poor market is the low pricing and large quantity of incoming goods.

Supplement to the Shanghai Newspaper

Comments

Selling Antiques 183

— Buddha

Selling antiques is originally a very good business. In Shanghai, there are many antique brokers who make a living from it every day, solving the four major elements of life: clothing, food, housing, and transportation.

Chinese antiques are naturally most abundant in the Forbidden City, so antique brokers often covet them and try to find ways to get them. Unexpectedly, a lawsuit was filed against the Forbidden City for allegedly selling antiques the other day. Also, yesterday, it was reported that a Peking University professor asked the central government not to move Forbidden City antiques, and a Shanghai University professor inquired about the truth of selling antiques. Although President Yi Peiji of the Executive Yuan declared that he had sold 310,000 yuan worth of furs and medicines, I feel that no matter what the president says, it still feels somewhat irresponsible.

[Mosquitoes don't bite yellow ducks without eggs,] is a seasoned folk saying. Rumors of the theft and sale of Forbidden City antiques have long been rife. Now that President Yi has been sued and has indeed admitted to selling 310,000 yuan worth of furs and medicines, I believe that the director of the Forbidden City Museum only has the right to preserve them, not the right to sell them. Even those who are slightly knowledgeable should understand their responsibilities.

[Don't adjust your shoes in a melon patch, don't fix your hat under a plum tree,] Forbidden City antiques are not private property. The president of the museum, being in a position of suspicion, should have reported to the National Government in advance if he wanted to sell antiques, and could only sell them after they were approved by the National Government Council. Now, there is no record of this procedure. Only after the people discovered the lawsuit did he admit to selling furs and medicines. This is the first suspicious point.

Rice, firewood, oil, and salt have market prices, but antiques do not. To show his sincerity, the president should have openly auctioned the antiques to avoid criticism. Although President Yi admitted to selling 310,000 yuan worth of furs and medicines, it is difficult to believe whether this is true. This is the second suspicious point.

The Forbidden City originally had many antiques, and furs and medicines are only two categories. Now that furs and medicines have been quietly sold, it is questionable whether other items can be fully preserved. Because there are many people who covet them, Forbidden City antiques have been stolen and stolen once or twice, so there is an organization for the Preservation Committee. Now, they have the name of preservation, but not the reality of preservation. What are they supposed to say?

Originally, I absolutely do not advocate preserving these antiques, because even more important and more precious things than antiques cannot be preserved in our country. Petty antiques are only playthings for adults and gentlemen. What is there to preserve? But if you want to sell them, don't sell them this way.

Mother Piao's Rice and Xin 184

— Chen Peizhi

Impoverished and desperate days, the hero's downfall is sad, people are cold and warm, but there is still a silk thread hanging under the city, why did he meet Mother Piao, a meal of grace was given early, when the withered tree meets spring, repay the mother with a thousand gold, a tall man of seven feet, ashamed to live in someone else's house, fortunately to be favored, women are better than men.

Feeling the Times

The mountains and rivers are broken like silk, the beacon smoke is bitter, the blood of Shenyang is tragically fresh, the seven-day cry of Qin will eventually be saved, the ten-year prosperity of Yue is not in vain, peace and harmony are all the plans of generals, reporting to the country should promote the whip of Zu Ti, to the warriors of Rehe, wave your spears to the east and don't delay.

Science

The Method of Making Silk from Cotton 185

— Jiang Tianlan

Although silk is a major product of our country, it is very expensive due to insufficient supply. Now someone has invented a kind of artificial silk whose luster and color are completely identical to real silk. Non-professionals can hardly distinguish between them. However, the texture is slightly looser than silk, and it can only be used as weft, not as warp.

Wet Silk Manufacturing Method: Immerse cotton in sulfuric acid and nitric acid. After it dries, dissolve it in alcohol and denaturant and burn it with heat. The ratio should be about 40 to 50 degrees on the soda water meter. Then, pour the cotton pulp into a sand hourglass tank to filter out the slag, and then use a machine to squeeze out the paste, place it in a large tube, and apply heavy pressure to force it to 40 to 50 degrees. The water has been completely clarified. Then, pour it into a small tube equipped with a Cook. The Cook hole is as small as a needle eye, so the silk that is squeezed out is no different from what silkworms spin. Then, immerse the silk in water to bleach out the smell of alcohol, and it becomes shiny and colorful silk.

Dry Silk Manufacturing Method: The method is the same as wet silk manufacturing. Since alcohol and denaturant are very dry, the silk is dry as soon as it is scooped out of the water, and it does not stick when it is shaken on the bobbin. However, sulfuric acid and nitric acid must be completely bleached out, otherwise they will ignite when touched by fire, causing great harm. The method of bleaching out the acid water is to simply place the silk in an ammonium sulfide solution and immediately remove it.

Society Improvement Discussion Group

Let's Talk About Improving Education 186

— Yi Yi

On August 16th, this association published an article by Mr. Xin Xi on improving education. After reading it, I couldn't help but feel something and would like to share my thoughts:

Yes, the relationship between education and society is very close. When education is developed, social causes will prosper and social happiness will progress. Otherwise, how can a country be developed and strong? Therefore, I believe that the reason why China is in such a bad state now is that the underdevelopment of education is at least a major cause.

The revival of Italy depended on education, the strength of Turkey depended on education, and in recent times, the dominance of Japan in the world has also depended on the merits of education. Moreover, history tells us that the development of education is indeed deeply related to the strength of the country, such as the Zhou, Han, and Song dynasties...

However, for more than ten years, the sages have been shouting to promote universal education, but to this day, they have not seen the popularization of education. The number of illiterate people still accounts for a very large majority. Where is the crux of the problem? I believe this is the corruption of education itself.

Let's not talk about social education or family education, let's just talk about school education!

Since the capitalist system invaded China, everything in Chinese society has become capitalist. Schools are institutions that hold a leading position in society, but how can they avoid this? Therefore, only the children of middle-class or upper-class families can inquire about the gates of noble (?) institutions.

I remember five years ago, a normal school student could pay a deposit of five or ten yuan and eat and study with peace of mind. But now it is not the case. Meal money must be subsidized at least four yuan, and textbooks, sports, library, medical, and experimental fees are two yuan each. Each semester, it cannot be done without twenty yuan. Thinking of the increasing collapse of rural society, one can only sigh helplessly.

Ah! Alas! Countless extraordinary talents have been buried here,

I feel that those who run education today cannot avoid having a kind of self-interest (in fact, everything is like this). Because of this, teachers with poorer skills can also earn a living by relying on powerful connections, and students with low academic ability can also be promoted step by step. Looking at any school, any school cannot avoid this kind of fact. How can the future of education be envisioned? How can the future of the country be optimistic?

I also feel that today's educators often do not pay attention to the four big characters of [learning for application][Although the formal aspects seem very neat and beautified, there should also be a good and practical guidance in the substantive aspects! Every year, a whole batch of graduates comes out, but as a result, many of them often suffer from unemployment. Why is this? It is because what is learned is not applied, and what is applied is not what is learned, that is, the graduating students cannot do their best for society, that is, the pointer of school education is not pointing to the needs of society.

Ten years of building up strength, ten years of teaching, saving the country depends on education, if education is not good, the country cannot be strong; this is my opinion on improving education, what do the wise think?

Sudden Change 188

— Xin Fu

Sunlight slanted through the glass window, making the delicate and tidy study seem even more arrogant and self-satisfied. With a face full of smiles, she fondled a letter just delivered by the postman, guessing at the deep affection and sweet tenderness that he used to convey in his letters. She imagined that the contents within were sure to be just as sweet. Thinking of this, two small dimples appeared on her plump cheeks.

Carefully, she tore open the letter. Two eyes, full of fervent passion, unwaveringly focused on line after line of blue ink on white paper. From the first page, the second page, the third page, she read it all. But her expression changed along with the progression of the letter. Her skin, which had been flushed with red, turned pale. The two dimples on her cheeks had long since disappeared. Her eyes, initially wide open, were now closed. Judging from the situation, she had clearly suffered a blow.

[Could I have misread it?] She muttered to herself, struggling back from her dazed state. She still didn't trust her first reading and unfolded the letter again to reread it.

M sister,

I myself can't believe I'm writing such a letter to you. I truly shouldn't be giving you a letter like this, but I can't help but write it to you. I know that when this letter passes your eyes, it will cause you sorrow and pain, or even inflict unimaginable distress upon you. M, I have sinned, but... alas! I hope you can understand my pain, which may even be greater than yours!

Haven't you been worried about my tyrannical family? Remember when I told you, [Even though my family is tyrannical, they will never be able to destroy our love. I will repay your love for me with my courage.] Alas! How long ago was that? My words have ended in tragic failure, and your worries have become reality. I have finally succumbed to my tyrannical family, and our love has ultimately been destroyed by them!

Originally, a man who yields to tyrannical power and abandons the one he loves is, to some extent, a weakling of humanity. Alas! I am indeed a weakling of humanity. (I can only admit this, otherwise, how else can I answer you?)

[If you don't agree to a marriage arranged by me and you, then, go be free! Start from now, I don't care about anything.]

This is the [declaration] issued by my father. I pity myself, a young man still halfway through my studies, and even more, I pity myself, a lonely young man who can only survive by relying on my father. I know that this kind of declaration is completely unreasonable, but how can I resist him? However, I still have to complete my studies, and I still want to live to serve society. I also thought that instead of committing suicide due to oppression, it would be better to yield and stay alive to be a servant of society. I can only sacrifice the happiness of my life, and only painfully give up your love for me.

M sister: I love you, alas! Today, I can no longer love you. I have deeply failed you! The past imaginations, the future sweetness, all have ended here.

I'm heartbroken! I can't think anymore! I can't write anymore. In this final moment, I must still beg you, please don't let this unfortunate event devastate your heart. You are an innocent and lively young girl, you should realize that your future holds much happiness. Just consider me an unfaithful man!

M: Perhaps you can just believe in the karma of marriage! In a past life, perhaps we didn't plant the [cause], so naturally we can't enjoy the right to the [effect]. Alas! [Deep love, but fate not sealed] should be interpreted this way. Wishing you health.

From M

She finished reading it for the second time. She no longer thought she had misread it, but felt that every word was like a hideous demon trying to claw at her heart. Due to the unexpected shock, she finally tasted the most unbearable pain in life. Two tears couldn't be held back and trickled down from the long lashes of her closing eyes.

No Way Out

The Woman Selling Rendan 189

— Tian Xiong

At that moment when the bright lights shone like daylight, along the bustling Fourth Avenue, in each restaurant, there was a fashionable woman in her twenties with bobbed hair, holding a large box of Rendan pills in her hand, peddling them to the diners. Looking at her beautiful face, though one couldn't say she was as beautiful as flowers or jade, she did possess a certain charm. However, her face seemed to hide a kind of sorrow.

The day before yesterday, I had dinner with a friend at the XX restaurant. Naturally, she came by as usual, holding her Rendan pills and offering them to us. I had drunk too much, and at that time, I could use some Rendan to freshen my mouth, so I bought a pack from her. Because I observed her demeanor and actions, which were unlike those of typical frivolous and unrestrained women, I wondered how she could be exposing herself in public, selling Rendan. Furthermore, observing the sorrow on her face, I was certain that there must be unspeakable suffering hidden within her heart. I firmly believed this and then aroused my curiosity, and unintentionally began to ask her about her background. She also thought that I was a kindred spirit, so she began to tell us about her life, as follows:

Alas, someone like me really has a bitter life. My husband has had no business for three years, and there is no one to take care of things in our hometown. In March this year, he came to Shanghai with me. He wanted to ask friends to find a position for him, but the friends couldn't find anything. Up until now, we really can't think of any way. That's why I came out to sell Rendan, she said, sobbing.

Then your husband is at home instead? I asked.

Yes! My husband is really a useless person. At first, he came out to sell them, but after selling for two days, he didn't sell a single pack. Seeing that our livelihood was about to be cut off, how could I just stay at home and do nothing? I had to come out and think of something myself. He's at home taking care of the children now, she said.

Then how much money can you make in a day? my friend asked her.

Alas! It's really pitiful. A few days ago, when it was hot, I could sell about one or two dollars a day. Now that the weather is getting cooler, I can't even sell one dollar. Sir, you think! In Shanghai, it costs money to sit and it costs money to stand. How can these meager profits be enough for our expenses? she said.

Then as the weather gradually gets cooler, the Rendan business will gradually become slow. For the three of you in Shanghai, even if you just talk about the lowest standard of living, you need no less than twenty or thirty dollars to maintain your life. How will you manage? I asked her again.

At this point, she began to sob again, answering me, Now we've lost everything. If we don't work for one day, we can't live for one day. At first, we wanted to rent a house to live in, but because we didn't have money, we had to temporarily borrow a small inn for half a dollar a day. If we still return to our hometown, we still have no way to think of, it's also just waiting to die, alas!

Then do you have anyone in your hometown? I continued to ask.

My mother-in-law passed away long ago, and my father-in-law also died last year. We don't have any daughters, younger brothers, or younger sisters. We used to run a foreign goods store in Huzhou, and we had a very good reputation. Later, the family property was completely squandered, all ruined by my father-in-law. Now we younger generations are suffering, I don't know what sins we committed in our past lives, alas! she answered.

After hearing the above words, I felt sympathy, and then comforted her with a few words. As I wanted to continue asking, she showed a distressed face because it had been too long, and bid us farewell. (Yet酬)

Market News 190

▲Luyin Plantation Promotes Fine Varieties of Seedlings The Luyin Plantation in Zhoupu, Pudong, was founded by Mr. Wu Jingcheng, an expert in arboriculture, and has been in operation for more than ten years. The jade dew peaches and other fruits produced there are delicious and sweet, far superior to those shipped from other provinces. Therefore, over the years, the supply has been unable to meet the demand. In order to popularize fine varieties, Mr. Wu has established a large nursery, specializing in the propagation of hundreds of thousands of fine seedlings, which are sold at low prices. The varieties are accurate, and success of each plant is guaranteed, to promote the spread of these fine fruits. A special Luyin publication has been printed, containing the business history and product names of the garden, which will be distributed to all sectors. If you wish to read it, you can send a letter to Luyin Plantation in Zhoupu, Pudong, to request it, free of charge, and it will be sent to you immediately.
